CHARLOTTE: "Perhaps you are reading too much into—" ELIZA @Image1: "I am reading exactly the right amount. It is a skill." All bipedal ANIMALS. NO humans. NO title cards. NO watermarks.

## EP.078 — Caroline on Eliza

**Images to upload (in this order):**

2. `characters/ELIZA_FETCHWORTH.png` → @Image2

**Prompt:**
EP.078 CAROLINE ON ELIZA. MUSIC: The Caroline Smile (#7). @Image1: CAROLINE BINGLEY (elegant Siamese cat, dark gown, long gloves, smile fully deployed, expressing sympathy for Eliza's education and connections — each compliment a precisely deployed scalpel). @Image2: ELIZA FETCHWORTH (Border Collie, Regency day gown, not wounded — genuinely amused, which is far worse for Caroline). Netherfield breakfast room. Caroline turns to Eliza with the smile deployed. Each expression of concern is a map of everything Eliza lacks. Eliza is amused. CAROLINE @Image1: "You must find Netherfield so... different from what you are accustomed to." ELIZA @Image2: "Different, yes. Quieter, certainly. One can hear every compliment land." CAROLINE @Image1 (smile not moving): "I only mean that you have managed very well, considering." ELIZA @Image2: "Considering what, precisely?" CAROLINE @Image1 (warmly): "Oh, everything. Everything." ELIZA @Image2 (to her toast, genuinely amused): "Extraordinary." All bipedal ANIMALS. NO humans. NO title cards. NO watermarks.

## EP.240 — Eliza Tells Darcy

**Images to upload (in this order):**

2. `characters/DARCY_PAWSWORTH.png` → @Image2

**Prompt:**
EP.240 ELIZA TELLS DARCY. MUSIC: 3 - Darcy Stare (sustained cello), grave. @Image1: ELIZA FETCHWORTH (Border Collie, Regency day gown, telling Darcy about Lydia and Wickham in halting words by the Pemberley lake — panic, not composure). @Image2: DARCY PAWSWORTH (sleek black cat, navy tailcoat, face closing like a door — very still, tail unmoving, whiskers unmoving — saying five words in a voice that is low and certain and already moving). Pemberley grounds, lake path. Key dialogue: ELIZA: "I should not have told you—" DARCY: "You told the right person. I will deal with this." ELIZA: "It is nothing to do with you—" DARCY (quietly, already certain): "It has everything to do with me. Go home, Miss Fetchworth." DARCY: "I will deal with this." All bipedal ANIMALS. NO humans. EP.266 JANE'S HOPE. MUSIC: 16 - Love Theme (tender strings), fragile. @Image1: JANE FETCHWORTH (Golden Retriever, quietly heartbroken, at an upstairs window — book open in her lap, page unturned for twenty minutes, ears lifting for every passing carriage). @Image2: ELIZA FETCHWORTH (Border Collie, Regency day gown, sitting beside her at the window, knowing exactly what she is watching for). Longbourn upstairs window, autumn afternoon. Key dialogue: JANE: "I am reading." ELIZA: "The page has not turned in half an hour." JANE: "I am reading very slowly." JANE (a long pause, eyes on the road): "He said my name the way — I heard it differently, is all." ELIZA (sitting beside her): "The road will not be empty forever." All bipedal ANIMALS. NO humans. ## EP.267 — Darcy and His Decision

**Images to upload (in this order):**
1. `characters/DARCY_PAWSWORTH.png` → @Image1

**Prompt:**
EP.267 DARCY AND HIS DECISION. MUSIC: 3 - Darcy Stare (sustained cello), resolved. @Image1: DARCY PAWSWORTH (sleek black cat, navy tailcoat, standing at the Pemberley study window in darkness — a single light, one lit window in the whole dark house, looking at the lake reflecting his light — past analysis, in the place where decision lives). Pemberley at night. Papers and a map on the desk behind him, ignored. He has decided. Key dialogue: DARCY (alone, to the dark grounds, quietly): "I have managed it wrong at every turn. I have been proud when I should have been humble, and silent when I should have spoken." (a pause) "I will not be silent again." (turns from the window) "Make ready the carriage for first light." All bipedal ANIMALS. NO humans. NO title cards. NO watermarks.

JANE: "She writes when she cannot win the argument. Which means she has failed to talk her brother out of something." ELIZA (quiet admiration): "Jane Fetchworth. You noticed." JANE: "I notice everything. I am simply more patient about it than you." All bipedal ANIMALS. NO humans. NO title cards. NO watermarks.

MUSIC: 17 - Gaston's Commentary. @Image1: GASTON CHEF (voice breaking slightly, surveying the room with pride, presenting a monumental four-tier cake decorated with sugar flowers and marzipan portraits). @Image2: LADY WOOFINGTON-BARKS (Pomeranian, architectural pink outfit, pearl necklace, standing hand to heart, proprietary love, as though she baked it herself). GASTON: "One hundred and forty sugar roses. Eight marzipan portraits -- I sat with a magnifying glass for six hours. You are welcome." LADY W-B: "I feel as though I made it myself." GASTON: "You did not." LADY W-B: "Spiritually." All bipedal ANIMALS. NO humans. NO title cards. NO watermarks.

EP.417 THE CAKE SITUATION. MUSIC: 11 - Scandal Sting. @Image1: GASTON CHEF (in doorway, plates in hand, covered in icing, watching in absolute slow horror, barely audible). @Image2: LADY WOOFINGTON-BARKS (Pomeranian, architectural pink outfit now completely covered in icing and marzipan, pearl necklace dripping, standing at the centre of the blast radius, deciding how to feel). The cake shifts, tilts, considers, then explodes horizontally; three tiers detonate outward; half the wedding breakfast wearing icing; Gaston's marzipan portraits destroyed. EP.420 THE CARRIAGES DEPART. MUSIC: 19 - Resolution Theme (full warm orchestra). @Image1: ELIZA FETCHWORTH (Border Collie, wedding gown, bonnet at its customary crooked angle, pausing on the carriage step, looking back at Longbourn, then turning to Darcy, allowing herself to be completely happy). @Image2: DARCY PAWSWORTH (sleek black cat, wedding tailcoat, fully thawed, warm, finally fully smiling — the first full smile in the entire series). @Image3: LORD BISCUIT-BOTTOMS (Basset Hound, best coat, crooked wig, on the steps, not waving, watching the carriage go, expression entirely his own). ELIZA: "Let's go." LADY W-B: "WRITE! WRITE IMMEDIATELY! EVERY DAY! WE WANT LETTERS!" All bipedal ANIMALS. NO humans. NO title cards. NO watermarks.
